A mysterious library appears in his mind. As long as it is something he has seen, regardless of whether it is a human or an object, a book on its weakness would be automatically compiled. Thus, he became formidable. &ldquo;Emperor Haotian, why don&rsquo;t you like to wear underwear?  $("#report_btn").on("click", function () {
 var modal = document.getElementById('myModal');
 console.log("xx");

 var ret = send_report(modal);
 if (ret) {
 modal.style.display = "none";
 }
 });
 function send_report(modal) {
 $("#report_error").html("");
 var $report_content = $("#report_content").val();
 var $report_episode_id = $("#report_episode_id").val();
 var $report_email = $("#report_email").val();
 var $report_film_id = $("#report_film_id").val();
 var $url = 'https://wuxiaworld.live/send_report.ajax';
 if ($report_content === '') {
 console.log("null content");
 $("#report_error").html("Please say somethings");
 return false;
 }

 if ($report_email !== '') {
 if (!validateEmail($report_email)) {
 console.log("email not valid");
 $("#report_error").html("Email is not valid");
 return false;
 }
 }

 var report = {};
 report['content'] = $report_content;
 report['episode_id'] = $report_episode_id;
 report['email'] = $report_email;
 report['film_id'] = $report_film_id;
 
 var data_param = {
 'report': report
 };
 
 $.ajax({
 url: $url,
 data: data_param,
 type: 'POST',
 success: function (data) {
 console.log(data);
 modal.style.display = "none";
 }
 });
 }

 function validateEmail(email) {
 var re = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
 return re.test(email);
 }
	function go_to_chapter(base_url) {
 var chapter_no = $("#go_to_chapter").val();
 if (chapter_no !== null&& chapter_no!=='') {
 
 var redirect_url = base_url +"/chapter-"+chapter_no;
 console.log(redirect_url);
 
 location.href = redirect_url;
 }

 }
	
	$(document).ready(function () {

 $("#go_to_chapter").keydown(function (e) {
 if (e.keyCode === 13) {
 var value = $(this).val();

 if (value !== null && value !== '')
 {

 var domain_url = $("#go_to_chapter").data("url");
 var $url = domain_url + "/chapter-" + value;
 window.location.href = $url;
 }
 }
 });
 });

	$(".flash-ads-close").on('click',function(){

// Get the modal
 var modal = document.getElementById('myModal');
 
 var span = document.getElementsByClassName("close")[0];
 

// When the user clicks on <span> (x), close the modal
 span.onclick = function () {
 modal.style.display = "none";
 }

// When the user clicks anywhere outside of the modal, close it
 window.onclick = function (event) {
 if (event.target == modal) {
 modal.style.display = "none";
 }
 }</script>
